        isEnabled: true,
        filter: null,
        numViews: 0,
        maxViews: 75,
        loading: false,
        init: function () {
            this.setFilter('all');
            const self = this;
            window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                self.onScroll();
            });
        },
        onScroll: function () {
            const self = this;
            const rect = self.$el.getBoundingClientRect();
            const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
            const threshold = rect.top + scrollTop + rect.height - window.innerHeight * 2;
            const scrollAmount = window.pageYOffset + window.innerHeight;
            if (scrollAmount > threshold) {
                self.next();
            }
        },
        setFilter: function (filter) {
            this.filter = filter;
            const self = this;
            this.listFiltered = [];
            this.listVisible = [];
            this.list.forEach(function (item) {
                if (self.filter === 'all') {
                    self.listFiltered.push(item);
                } else if (self.filter === 'winner' && item.result) {
                    self.listFiltered.push(item);
                } else if (self.filter === 'loser' && !item.result) {
                    self.listFiltered.push(item);
                }
            });
            this.next();
            setTimeout(function () {
                self.onScroll();
            })
        },
        next() {
            if (this.loading) {
                return;
            }
            this.loading = true;
            for (let i = 0; i < this.maxViews; i++) {
                const item = this.listFiltered.shift();
                if (item) {
                    this.listVisible.push(item);
                }
            }
            const self = this;
            setTimeout(function () {
                self.loading = false;
            })
        },
        getProfileLink: function (nicename) {
            return 'https://sv.j-cg.com/user' + '/' + nicename;
        },
        getClassName: function (result) {
            if (this.bracketPublished) {
                return (result) ? 'entry winner' : 'entry loser';
            }
            return 'entry';
        },
        getClanImage: function (clanId) {
            return this.clanImages[clanId];
        },
        getDeckUrl: function (clanId, hash) {
	    if( clanId > 10 ){
                return 'https://shadowverse-portal.com/deck_co/' + hash;
	    }else{
                return 'https://shadowverse-portal.com/deck/' + hash;
	    }
        },
    }
</script>
